        <h2><span class="small">Guiding Your Journey</span> From Start to Finish</h2>
        <p>NYBG can help patients at every step of their journey including pre, and post weight loss. For men interested in bariatric surgery, they can help you select the right procedure. After you have lost excess weight our surgeons can help sculpt your shape. This may include gynecomastia, liposuctions, or procedures to remove excess skin in order to enhance your features.</p>

          <h2><span class="small">Patient Journeys</span></h2>
          <h2>Caitlyn</h2>
          <p>After losing all the weight, I had excess skin, a lot of rashes, and my clothes didn't fit properly. Dr. Small made me feel incredibly comfortable, he was thorough about what to expect and what results would be best for me. My results are incredible. When I look in the mirror, I still can't believe it's me. They removed 10 1/2 lbs of excess skin. My life has forever changed.</p>
        </div>

        <h2><span class="small">Helping Balance Your Shape With</span> Breast Procedures</h2>
        <p>There are many reasons you may be dissatisfied with the appearance of your breasts, and this can have a subtle or profound impact on numerous areas of your life. Breasts define upper body shape and dictate the range of clothing that fits and looks best. Having the breasts you feel make you more attractive or shapely is often a life-changing event.&nbsp;</p>
        <p>Whether your breasts need correction due to age, pregnancy, genetics, or injury, our full range of cosmetic procedures can result in a stunning improvement that lifts your spirits and makes you feel shapely and attractive.
